DROP TABLE MEMBER CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE SELLER CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE SELLERBOARD CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE TALENT1 CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE TALENT2 CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE DEALMANAGER CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE INCOME CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE CASH CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE COUPON CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE REQUEST CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE BOARDCOMMENT CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_MNO;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_SENO;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_SSNO;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_RNO;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_DMCODE;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_PAYNO;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_ICCODE;
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_CNO;

--멤버 시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_MNO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1;

--판매자 시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_SENO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

--판매서비스 번호
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_SSNO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

--댓글 번호
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_CNO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

-- 문의글 번호(RNO) 시퀀스 --
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_RNO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

-- 거래 건 번호(DMCODE) 시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_DMCODE
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

--캐시 시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_PAYNO
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1;

-- 수익 관련 시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_ICCODE
START WITH 1
INCREMENT BY 1
NOCYCLE
NOCACHE;

CREATE TABLE MEMBER(
       MNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,
       EMAIL VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
       PASSWORD VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
       USERNAME VARCHAR2(18) NOT NULL,
       NICKNAME VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
       PHONE VARCHAR2(13),
       USER_SSN VARCHAR2(14),
       ENROLLDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
       EMAILYN VARCHAR2(1) DEFAULT '0',
       CASH NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
       ISSELLER CHAR DEFAULT 'N',
       PROFILEIMAGE VARCHAR2(300),
       COUPON VARCHAR2(100),
       ISALIVE CHAR DEFAULT 'Y',
       ISVALID CHAR DEFAULT 'Y',
       ISADMIN CHAR DEFAULT 'N'
);

CREATE TABLE TALENT1(
    CATEGORY1_CODE VARCHAR2(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    CATEGORY1_NAME VARCHAR2(50) UNIQUE
);

CREATE TABLE TALENT2(
    CATEGORY2_CODE VARCHAR2(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    CATEGORY2_NAME VARCHAR2(50) UNIQUE
);

--판매자
CREATE TABLE SELLER(
    SNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                 --판매자번호(PK)
    MNO NUMBER UNIQUE,                      --회원 번호(FK)
    CALLTIME VARCHAR2(100),                 --연락가능시간
    BANKNAME VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,         --계좌은행
    BANKNUMBER VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,       --계좌번호
    INCOME NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                --수익금
    CAREERDATE1 VARCHAR2(100),              --경력기간1
    CAREERDATE2 VARCHAR2(100),              --경력기간2   
    CAREERDATE3 VARCHAR2(100),              --경력기간3
    CAREER1 VARCHAR2(100),                   --경력사항1
    CAREER2 VARCHAR2(100),                   --경력사항2
    CAREER3 VARCHAR2(100),                   --경력사항3
    CERTIFICAT1 VARCHAR2(100),               --자격증1
    CERTIFICAT2 VARCHAR2(100),               --자격증2
    CERTIFICAT3 VARCHAR2(100),               --자격증2
    INTROTEXT VARCHAR2(500),                --소개글
    CPCOUNT NUMBER DEFAULT 0,              --작업 완료 건수
    SEVALUATION  NUMBER DEFAULT 0,          --판매자 평점
    CONSTRAINT FK_MNO FOREIGN KEY(MNO) REFERENCES MEMBER(MNO) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

--판매게시물
CREATE TABLE SELLERBOARD (
      BNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                                   --판매글 번호(PK)
      SNO NUMBER NOT NULL,                                      --판매자 번호(FK)
      BTITLE VARCHAR2(500) NOT NULL,                            --제목
      BCONTENT VARCHAR2(4000) NOT NULL,                         --상세 설명
      ERECONTENT VARCHAR2(1500),                                --수정 및 재진행 안내
      REQUEST VARCHAR2(1500),                                   --작업 전 요청사항
      CATEGORY1_CODE VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,                     --상위 카테고리
      CATEGORY2_CODE VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,                     --하위 카테고리
      PRICE NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                                   --가격
      BEVALUATION NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                              --평점
      IMAGES VARCHAR2(1000),                                    --이미지들
      EDITABLECOUNT NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                           --수정 횟수
      DUEDATE NUMBER NOT NULL,                                  --작업 기간
      SPEED NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                                   --빠른 작업(옵션)
      extradate1 VARCHAR2(10) DEFAULT 0,                              --빠른 작업 일수
      PLUSEDIT NUMBER DEFAULT 0,                                --추가 수정(옵션)
      extradate2 VARCHAR2(10) DEFAULT 0,                              --추가 수정 회수
      AD VARCHAR2(1) DEFAULT 'Y' CHECK (AD IN ('Y', 'N')),      --광고여부[Y,N]
      ADEXPIRE NUMBER,                                          --광고 만료일
      BDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,                               --작성일
      STATE VARCHAR2(60) DEFAULT 'B1' CHECK (STATE IN ('B1','B2','B3','B4')),--상태
      -- B1 : 승인대기중, B2:승인, B3:판매중지, B4:비승인
      
      CONSTRAINT FK_SNO FOREIGN KEY(SNO) REFERENCES SELLER(SNO) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT FK_C1CODE FOREIGN KEY(CATEGORY1_CODE) REFERENCES TALENT1(CATEGORY1_CODE) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT FK_C2CODE FOREIGN KEY(CATEGORY2_CODE) REFERENCES TALENT2(CATEGORY2_CODE) ON DELETE CASCADE
      
);

-- 댓글
CREATE TABLE BOARDCOMMENT (
      CNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,
      BNO NUMBER NOT NULL,
      CCONTENT VARCHAR2(2000) NOT NULL,
      CWRITER VARCHAR2(1500) NOT NULL,
      CDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
      REF_CNO NUMBER,
      CLEVEL NUMBER,
      CONSTRAINT FK_CWRITER FOREIGN KEY(CWRITER) REFERENCES MEMBER(email) ON DELETE SET NULL
);

-- 거래과정 테이블
CREATE TABLE DEALMANAGER(
    DMCODE NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,      --거래코드
    BNO NUMBER,             --게시글코드
    MNO NUMBER,               --구매자코드
    SNO NUMBER,           --판매자코드
    PRICE NUMBER,
    PROGRESS VARCHAR2(30) DEFAULT '진행중' NOT NULL, --진행사항
    DEALDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL, --거래날짜
    EDITCOUNT NUMBER DEFAULT 0,             --수정횟수
    COMPLETEYN CHAR DEFAULT 'N' CHECK(COMPLETEYN IN('Y','N')),  --완료여부
    COMPLETEDATE DATE,                          --완료날짜
    CONSTRAINT FK_DMBNO FOREIGN KEY(BNO) REFERENCES SELLERBOARD(BNO) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT FK_DMMNO FOREIGN KEY(MNO) REFERENCES MEMBER(MNO) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT FK_DMSNO FOREIGN KEY(SNO) REFERENCES SELLER(SNO) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- 수익관리 테이블
CREATE TABLE INCOME(
    ICCODE VARCHAR(30) PRIMARY KEY,
    SNO NUMBER,
    BNO NUMBER,
    ICMONEY NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    ICDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
    ICHISTORY VARCHAR(20) CHECK(ICHISTORY IN('수익','출금')),
    CONSTRAINT FK_ICBNO FOREIGN KEY(BNO) REFERENCES SELLERBOARD(BNO) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT FK_ICSNO FOREIGN KEY(SNO) REFERENCES SELLER(SNO) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- 캐시
CREATE TABLE CASH(
    PAYNO NUMBER UNIQUE,            --결제코드
    MNO NUMBER,                     --멤버코드(FK)
    PAYP NUMBER NOT NULL,           --결제금액
    PAYDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,   --결제일
    CLASSIFY VARCHAR2(10) CHECK (CLASSIFY IN('충전','사용','환불')),
    
    CONSTRAINT FK_PAYMNO FOREIGN KEY(MNO) REFERENCES MEMBER(MNO)
);


-- 쿠폰관리
CREATE TABLE COUPONMANAGE(
    CPNO NUMBER,                     --쿠폰코드
    VALIDDATE DATE,                 --유효기간
    REGISTDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,--쿠폰등록일
    MNO NUMBER UNIQUE,              --멤버코드(FK)
    CONSTR VARCHAR2(90),            --적용조건
    
    CONSTRAINT FK_MNO FOREIGN KEY(MNO) REFERENCES MEMBER(MNO) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT FK_CPCONSTR FOREIGN KEY(CONSTR) REFERENCES COUPON(CONSTR) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT FT_CPNO FOREIGN KEY(CPNO) REFERENCES COUPONMANAGE(CPNO) ON DELETE CASCADE
);


-- 쿠폰
CREATE TABLE COUPON(
    CPNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,        --쿠폰코드(FK)
    CPNAME VARCHAR2(90) NOT NULL,   --쿠폰명
    DISCOUNT NUMBER NOT NULL,       --할인금액
    CONSTR VARCHAR2(90)             --적용조건
);


-- 1:1 문의(REQUEST)  --
CREATE TABLE REQUEST(
    RNO NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,
    EMAIL VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    NICKNAME VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    RTITLE VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL,
    RCONTENT VARCHAR2(3000) NOT NULL,
    RDATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
    REPLY VARCHAR2(2) DEFAULT 'N',
    REPLYTITLE VARCHAR2(1000),
    REPLYCONTENT VARCHAR2(3000)
);
